261→\t\tisConsole = cfg.Log.Encoding == config.LogEncodingConsole\n   262→\n   263→\t\tupdateAvailable bool\n   264→\t\tcv, lv          semver.Version\n   265→\t)\n   266→\n   267→\tif isConsole {\n
